+0000","feedId":44,"bgimg":"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/36/Show-Empathy-Step-1-Version-8.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-1-Version-8.jpg","linkMd5":"80748a33d148a074bf826cdca0a61af9","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn3@2020_1/2020/10/12/17-04-45-152_29b99a182c9e1196.webp","destWidth":728,"destHeight":546,"sourceBytes":69988,"destBytes":37688,"author":"","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/36/Show-Empathy-Step-1-Version-8.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-1-Version-8.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn3@2020_1/2020/10/12/17-04-45-152_29b99a182c9e1196.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/59/Show-Empathy-Step-2-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-2-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn100@2020_1/2020/10/12/17-04-48-500_e406c5d9ac6c57b3.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/cf/Show-Empathy-Step-3-Version-8.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-3-Version-8.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn48@2020_2/2020/10/12/17-04-47-194_347692c130b2e29d.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8a/Show-Empathy-Step-4-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-4-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn62@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-47-492_9e2ac8c4f1fb3dbe.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c2/Show-Empathy-Step-5-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-5-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn43@2020_5/2020/10/12/17-04-48-265_0cb55a2d036ff514.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/69/Show-Empathy-Step-6-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-6-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn88@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-47-259_a5f73013a4bc58fa.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/97/Show-Empathy-Step-7-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-7-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn76@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-47-209_e36d244525355807.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/be/Show-Empathy-Step-8-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-8-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn52@2020_4/2020/10/12/17-04-48-843_d797794c04c0c4ce.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/5/57/Show-Empathy-Step-9-Version-6.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-9-Version-6.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn67@2020_5/2020/10/12/17-04-48-366_936d807354da4a12.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/6d/Show-Empathy-Step-10-Version-7.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-10-Version-7.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx27/cdn95@2020_2/2020/10/12/17-04-48-358_a3753bebe0d18998.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/cf/Show-Empathy-Step-11-Version-6.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-11-Version-6.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn94@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-47-278_8e8e934c668f58c4.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/2b/Show-Empathy-Step-12-Version-6.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-12-Version-6.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn64@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-49-759_1be023040d293265.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a6/Show-Empathy-Step-13-Version-6.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-13-Version-6.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn87@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-47-263_b4ced78ca142e64b.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/62/Show-Empathy-Step-14.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-14.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn11@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-49-352_e3b5b8951bb5ac8f.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Show-Empathy-Step-15.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-15.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn31@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-49-444_2d6bc5e7a6f01d71.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e5/Show-Empathy-Step-16.jpg/aid698460-v4-728px-Show-Empathy-Step-16.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn28@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-47-299_d85e62c49e8ae7a7.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602522267280},{"createdTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:27","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:27","title":"How to Make a Brochure Using Google Docs","link":"https://www.wikihow.com/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs","description":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\">\n <p>This wikiHow teaches you how to create and print a brochure in Google Docs. The most common brochure type is a tri-fold brochure, which may also be known as a pamphlet. Although Google Docs doesn't have a tri-fold brochure template, it's pretty easy to create your own. If you're not concerned with the format and just want to make a simple two-page brochure, you can use one of Google Doc's free business brochure templates. </p> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1\" title=\"Edit section: Steps\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Steps\">Steps</span></h2> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\" title=\"Edit section: Tri-Fold Brochure\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Tri-Fold-Brochure\">Tri-Fold Brochure</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Go to <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external free\" href=\"https://docs.google.com\">https://docs.google.com</a> in your browser. If you're not already <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Log-in-to-Google\" title=\"Log in to Google\">signed into Google Docs</a>, follow the on-screen instructions to sign in now with your Google Account. \n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-1-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 1 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e5/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-1-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-1-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Before you get started, decide what you want your tri-fold brochure to look like. Brochures come in many shapes and sizes. Think about how many pages you want your brochure to have and the size of each page.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Click to create a blank document. It's the large rainbow plus sign in the top-left area of the page.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-12-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 12 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c3/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-12-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-12-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>To name the file, click the \"Untitled Document\" textbox in the upper-left corner of the window, then enter a type in a title for your brochure.\n     <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n      <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-13-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 13 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a6/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-13-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-13-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n     </div></li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Click the menu and select . This is where you can set up the dimensions of the file.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-14-Version-7.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 14 Version 7.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/09/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-14-Version-7.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-14-Version-7.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Click the radio button next to \"Landscape.\" This changes the page orientation of the document to landscape so you can fold the brochure properly.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-4-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 4 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/26/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-4-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-4-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Set the margins as \"0.25\" and click . The margins are on the right side of the window. This gives you more space for images and text. \n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-16-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 16 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/8b/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-16-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-16-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Create a three-column table. You'll need to create three columns on both sides of the page so you can fold it into thirds. To do this:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-6-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 6 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/ca/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-6-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-6-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Click the <b>Insert</b> menu at the top of Docs.</li> \n    <li>Select the <b>Table</b> menu.</li> \n    <li>Drag your mouse so only the top three squares are highlighted. Each of the squares will represent a column in your brochure.</li> \n    <li>When you see the new table, press the <b>Enter</b> or <b>Return</b> key repeatedly to extend the columns to the bottom of the second page. Since you're making a tri-fold brochure, you'll want your columns to line up on both sides of the sheet. The idea is that you'll see three vertical columns on both sides of the page (you can hide the actual lines later). Although you haven't added data yet, this gives you some visual table lines to work with.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Familiarize yourself with the tri-fold layout. You should now have 2 pages with three columns each. Since you'll be folding the brochure along the lines, the layout will look like this:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-8.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 7 Version 8.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/74/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-8.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-8.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li><b>Page 1 (the \"outside\" page):</b> Inside flap (this part folds in) | Back Cover | Front Cover</li> \n    <li><b>Page 2 (the \"inside\" page):</b> Other side of inside flap | Inside of Back Cover | Inside of Front Cover</li> \n    <li>It might be more helpful to visualize if you take a sheet of paper, draw column markers, and then fold it in this order: \n     <ul>\n      <li>Fold the left panel down (behind the cover).</li> \n      <li>Fold the right panel (the cover) behind so it covers the other panels (the back cover will now be at the top).</li> \n      <li>Flip the folded brochure over so the cover page is on top (and opens like a book).</li>\n     </ul></li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Design the front cover. The front cover of the tri-fold brochure will be the rightmost column on the first page (column 3).<sup id=\"_ref-1\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 1\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs#_note-1\">[1]</a></sup> The design of your cover is up to you, but here are a few ideas to get you started:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-8-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 8 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ab/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-8-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-8-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Type your desired title at the top (or anywhere, really) of column 3. Just click the mouse cursor in the column and start typing. To stylize the text, highlight what you've typed and use the text style menus and buttons that run along the top of the document. \n     <ul>\n      <li>For example, you can select a style by clicking the menu that says <b>Normal text</b> and choosing an option. You can also change the font face, size, weight, and even color.</li> \n      <li>It's common to center the title. To do so, highlight it and click the button of 4 centered lines in the toolbar.</li>\n     </ul></li> \n    <li>A strong cover image is important to illustrate the purpose of the brochure, as well as draw the interest of readers. To add an image, click the desired location, click the <b>Insert</b> menu, select <b>Image</b>, navigate to the image's location, select it, and then click <b>Open</b>. \n     <ul>\n      <li>Drag the blue anchors around the image's edges to reside if it desired.</li>\n     </ul></li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Design the back cover. This is the center panel of page one, so it's directly to the left of the front cover. Brochure back panels often include contact information, credits, and closing statements. Occasionally back panels are even designed as mailing panels so you can mail it without an envelope.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-9-Version-7.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 9 Version 7.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/39/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-9-Version-7.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-9-Version-7.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>It's a good idea to make the back panel as vibrant as the front so it draws attention to matter where the brochure is placed.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Create the first inside panel. Now that you're done with the two covers, it's time to add the rest of the content. Page 1 of the brochure will be inside the front cover, which is the third column on the second page. Since this is usually where you'll introduce the product or service, it'll probably be a little more text-heavy than the front or back covers.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-10-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 10 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/6e/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-10-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-10-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>When you open a tri-fold brochure, you'll see a flap on the right side that can be opened up. That flap, which is the leftmost column of Page 1, should contain stand-alone information, such as an ad, or special offer.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Add content to the rest of your brochure. Since you've introduced the product or service in the first column of page 2, you can continue adding content to the remaining pages. Since you already know how to add text and photos, check out these tips for more in-depth text formatting:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-11-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 11 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/b0/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-11-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-11-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>If you add images, you'll want to make them work with the text by setting up wrapping. Click the image after inserting it, and then click one of the three wrap icons below it. \n     <ul>\n      <li>Inline (icon 1) means the image will be added as part of the text, causing the image to shift when text is added or deleted. This is not recommended as it can cause formatting issues in the case of a brochure.</li> \n      <li>Wrap text (icon 2) allows text to flow around and to the side of an image. This is a good option for the inside of a brochure when you have small images amongst paragraph text.</li> \n      <li>Break text (icon 3) means the text will stop above and continue below the image. This is a good option for tri-fold brochures as the columns are small and don't have a lot of space for text to go around the image.</li>\n     </ul></li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Hide the table outline to see the final product. Now that you've designed your brochure, you can get rid of those black guidelines. Here's how:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-12-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 12 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/49/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-12-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-12-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Click any blank area inside any column to select the table.</li> \n    <li>Right-click any blank area inside the table and select <b>Table properties</b>.</li> \n    <li>Change the default line size (1pt) to <b>0pt</b>.</li> \n    <li>Click <b>OK</b>.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Print the brochure on a duplex printer. Since the inside and outside pages of the brochure technically span two separate pages, you'll need to print both pages together double-sided. Here's how to this in Google Docs:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-13-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 13 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/61/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-13-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-13-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"547\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Click the <b>File</b> menu and select <b>Print</b>.</li> \n    <li>Select your printer from the \"Destination\" menu.</li> \n    <li>Select how many copies to print (start with one just to make sure you like what you see).</li> \n    <li>Expand the <b>More settings</b> menu.</li> \n    <li>In the \"Two-sided\" section, check the box next to \"Print on both sides,\" and then select <b>Flip on short edge</b> from the drop-down menu. This is because the file is in landscape mode—flipping on the long side would make the inside print upside-down.<sup id=\"_ref-2\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 2\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs#_note-2\">[2]</a></sup></li>\n   </ul></li>\n </ol> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3\" title=\"Edit section: Two Page Brochure\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Two-Page-Brochure\">Two Page Brochure</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Go to <a target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer noopener\" class=\"external free\" href=\"https://docs.google.com\">https://docs.google.com</a> in your browser. If you're not already signed into Google Docs, follow the on-screen instructions to sign in now with your Google Account. \n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-1-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 1 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e5/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-1-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-1-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Although Google Docs has a brochure template, it's not the typical tri-fold style you may be expecting. Still, it'll work in a pinch when you need to get people the information they need.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Click . It's in the top-right side of the Google Docs page. This expands a set of pre-made templates you can use to create documents.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-2-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 2 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/9a/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-2-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-2-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Click a brochure template in the \"Work\" section. There are two brochure templates in the \"Work\" section—one called \"Modern Writer\" (a travel-oriented template) and another called \"Geometric\" (a basic product template). Click the template that best suits your needs.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-4-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 4 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/02/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-4-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-4-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Replace the placeholder text with your own text. You'll notice all the text in the brochure is generic, like \"Your Company\" and \"Product Brochure.\" The blocks of text of placeholder text beginning with \"Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet\". Triple-click some placeholder text to highlight it, and then start typing your own content. \n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-5-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 5 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/ad/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-5-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-5-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Replace an image. Brochure templates come with images pre-inserted, but you can easily replace them with images of your own without messing up the format. Here's how:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-6-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 6 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/e/e6/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-6-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-6-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Click the image to select it.</li> \n    <li>Right-click the image.</li> \n    <li>Select <b>Replace image</b>.</li> \n    <li>Click <b>Upload from computer</b> (or select another location, like Google Drive or Google Photos).</li> \n    <li>Select the replacement image and click <b>Open</b>.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Change the image size if needed. With the image still select, click and drag the blue squares on the corners of the image to resize the image.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-7.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 7 Version 7.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3e/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-7.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-7.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>If you upload an image that is smaller than needed, making it bigger may cause it to look pixilated and fuzzy.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Reformat your text if needed. If you want to make text bigger or smaller, use a different font, or use a different color, you can apply your preferred changes by highlighting the text that you want to change and then clicking an option in the menu bar at the top of the page.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 7 Version 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/b9/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-5.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-7-Version-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>For example, you can make the text bold by highlighting it and then clicking <b>B</b> at the top of the page. Or you can use the \"Font\" drop-down menu to change the font.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Print the brochure. Use the following steps to print the brochure:\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-9-Version-6.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Make a Brochure Using Google Docs Step 9 Version 6.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/cc/Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-9-Version-6.jpg/aid6434720-v4-728px-Make-a-Brochure-Using-Google-Docs-Step-9-Version-6.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Click <b>File</b> in the upper-right corner of the menu bar.</li> \n    <li>Click <b>Print</b>.</li>\n   </ul></li>\n 01:04:27","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:27","title":"How to Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets","link":"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets","description":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\">\n <p>The new hair color you picked is beautiful, but that spot on the carpet where it dripped? Not so much. Permanent hair dye is relatively easy to remove from carpet if you act quickly. But even if you don't notice a spot until after it's already set in, you can still get it up and have your carpet looking like new — it just might take a little more effort. While you might be able to buy a commercial carpet cleaner that removes hair dye, you can easily make a solution yourself with a few basic household ingredients. </p> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1\" title=\"Edit section: Steps\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Steps\">Steps</span></h2> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\" title=\"Edit section: Fresh Spills\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Fresh-Spills\">Fresh Spills</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Soak up as much liquid as possible with a clean cloth. Before you start cleaning the spill, press on it with a cloth to dry it out as much as possible. Fold the cloth over and press again until there is no visible liquid on the carpet.<sup id=\"_ref-1\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 1\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-1\">[1]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-1-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 1 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/76/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-1-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-1-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Don't rub on the dye or scrub it — you'll cause it to spread and become more deeply absorbed in the carpet, which will make it harder to get out. You also risk damaging the carpet fibers.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Mix dishwashing liquid, white vinegar, and water in a shallow bowl. Use the formula of of dishwashing liquid and of white vinegar to of water to make your cleaning solution. Just stir the ingredients around a little to mix it together.<sup id=\"_ref-2\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 2\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-2\">[2]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-2-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 2 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/df/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-2-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-2-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>The basic formula should provide enough cleaning solution for you to clean the spot. If you have a larger spill, though, you might want to mix more.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Dip a clean, white cloth in the solution and dab it repeatedly on the spot. Get your cloth damp, then press it on the dye spot. Lift, then press again. Continue dipping your cloth into the solution and pressing it back onto the spot, watching the dye come up from the carpet onto the cloth.<sup id=\"_ref-3\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 3\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-3\">[3]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-3-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 3 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/16/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-3-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-3-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Using a white cloth means you don't have to worry about any color from the cloth transferring to your carpet. It also makes it easier to see the dye you're pulling up.</li> \n    <li>Be careful not to rub the mixture into the carpet — you can damage the carpet fibers or cause the dye to become more deeply embedded in the carpet, which will make it more difficult to remove.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Rinse the affected area with cool water. When you can't see any more dye in the carpet, pour a little water over the spot to rinse out the solution. Then, continue blotting with your cloth or with a dry sponge.<sup id=\"_ref-4\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 4\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-4\">[4]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-4-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 4 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/9/93/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-4-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-4-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>You might need to pour more water to rinse again — this is up to you. If you still smell vinegar in the carpet, it's a good idea to rinse it again.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Dry the carpet with cool air or a sponge. Blot up the excess water. From there, you can usually just let the carpet air dry — it shouldn't take very long. If the spot was in a high-traffic area and you want it to dry faster, you might press it with a dry sponge to soak up more of the moisture.<sup id=\"_ref-5\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 5\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-5\">[5]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-5-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 5 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/87/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-5-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-5-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>You can also set up a fan to blow on the damp carpet.</li>\n   </ul></li>\n </ol> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3\" title=\"Edit section: Deep-Set Stains\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Deep-Set-Stains\">Deep-Set Stains</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Soak the stain in a dishwashing detergent and vinegar solution. In a shallow bowl, mix of dishwashing liquid and of white vinegar with of water. Soak a cloth or sponge in the solution and squeeze it over the stain to soak the carpet.<sup id=\"_ref-6\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 6\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-6\">[6]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-6-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 6 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/3b/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-6-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-6-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>You could also pour the solution over the stain slowly to flood the area. This might work better if the stain is larger.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Dab at the stain with a clean, white cloth every 5 minutes for a half-hour. Set a timer for 30 minutes. Every 5 minutes, take your white cloth and dab at the stain. If the area seems to be drying out, you might want to squeeze on a little more cleaning solution.<sup id=\"_ref-7\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 7\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-7\">[7]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-7-Version-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 7 Version 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/2/2d/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-7-Version-2.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-7-Version-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Dabbing at the stain helps the cleaning solution soak more deeply into the carpet fibers. Don't scrub, though — you could damage your carpet.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Rinse the stain with cool water. After your 30 minutes is up, pour cold water on the stain to rinse off the cleaning solution. Use a sponge or clean cloth to soak up the excess water. You might still be able to see the stain, but it should be less noticeable, at least.<sup id=\"_ref-8\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 8\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-8\">[8]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-8-Version-3.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 8 Version 3.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c8/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-8-Version-3.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-8-Version-3.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>If you can't tell much difference, you might want to do another 30 minutes with the cleaning solution, just to get more of the dye out of the surface.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Blot remnants of the stain with rubbing alcohol. Use a clean, white cloth or a cotton swab (depending on the size of the stain that's left) to blot rubbing alcohol directly on the stain. Dab at the stain gently until it disappears.<sup id=\"_ref-9\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 9\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-9\">[9]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-9.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 9.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1b/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-9.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-9.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>A deeper-set stain might take a little more work to get rid of, so expect to dab it more than once. If it seems like the rubbing alcohol isn't affecting the stain at all, though, you might have to try another solution to get rid of it.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Rinse the area with cold water to get rid of the rubbing alcohol. Pour a little water on the area to rinse the rubbing alcohol away. Soak up the excess moisture with a clean, dry cloth or sponge.<sup id=\"_ref-10\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 10\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-10\">[10]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-10.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 10.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/0/0f/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-10.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-10.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>If you were only treating a small area with alcohol on a cotton swab, you might not need to pour water on the area to rinse it. Just squeeze water out of a sponge or cloth.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Sponge or blot excess moisture from the carpet. Use a dry sponge or dry, white cloth to soak up the excess moisture in the carpet. While the carpet will still be damp after you do this, you can usually just let it air dry.<sup id=\"_ref-11\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 11\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-11\">[11]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-11.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 11.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/33/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-11.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-11.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Put an electric fan on the floor so that it's blowing on the spot if you want it to dry out faster.</li>\n   </ul></li>\n </ol> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4\" title=\"Edit section: Stubborn Spots\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Stubborn-Spots\">Stubborn Spots</span></h3> \n <ol>\n  <li>Make an ammonia and dishwashing liquid solution in a shallow bowl. Mix of dishwashing liquid and of ammonia in of warm water. You might want to wear a face covering if ammonia fumes bother you.<sup id=\"_ref-12\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 12\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-12\">[12]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-12.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 12.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/d/d3/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-12.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-12.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Mix this solution in a well-ventilated area to cut down on the fumes.</li> \n    <li>Don't mix any other chemicals in this solution, especially bleach — the fumes are toxic.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Apply the solution to a small area to test if it damages your carpet. Find a small, obscure area of your carpet where no one would notice if it was damaged. Dip a cotton swab in your ammonia solution and apply it to that area. If it singes or destroys the carpet fibers, don't use this solution to try to clean the stain.<sup id=\"_ref-13\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 13\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-13\">[13]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-13.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 13.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/cc/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-13.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-13.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Ammonia is effective at getting out hair dye, but it damages wool. Since you probably don't know if your carpet has any wool in it, use this test to make sure the solution won't damage your carpet. Better safe than sorry!</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Dab the solution all over the stained area. Dip a clean, white cloth in the solution, then dab it over the stubborn stain. Repeat until the stained portion of the carpet is completely covered in the solution. Don't pour the solution on the spot — too much ammonia could ruin your carpet.<sup id=\"_ref-14\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 14\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-14\">[14]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-14.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 14.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/80/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-14.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-14.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>It's a good idea to wear plastic gloves to protect your hands from the ammonia.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Blot the solution every 5 minutes for at least half an hour. Set a timer and come back every 5 minutes. Dip your cloth in the solution and re-apply it, dabbing at the stain. You should notice the stain start to come up from the carpet. If the stain isn't completely gone after a half an hour, you can keep doing it for longer if it appears to be working.<sup id=\"_ref-15\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 15\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-15\">[15]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-15.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 15.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c8/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-15.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-15.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Each time you come back to blot the solution, look at the condition of the carpet. If the carpet fibers in the spot look damaged compared to the surrounding carpet, rinse the ammonia out before it gets worse.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Rinse the carpet with cold water. Pour cold water on the carpet to rinse the ammonia out, immediately soaking it up with a clean, dry cloth. You'll probably need to rinse it several times.<sup id=\"_ref-16\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 16\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-16\">[16]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-16.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 16.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/31/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-16.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-16.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>It can be hard to tell, but keep rinsing until you can't smell any ammonia fumes coming from the carpet.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Dry the carpet with a fan or dry cloth. Use a dry cloth or a dry sponge to help soak up the excess moisture on the carpet. Even after doing this, leave a fan blowing on the spot for at least an hour, or until the carpet feels completely dry.<sup id=\"_ref-17\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 17\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-17\">[17]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-17.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 17.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a1/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-17.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-17.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Once the carpet is dry, check its condition. If the stain is gone, congratulations! If the carpet looks bleached-out, you might want to use a fabric pen to fill it back in so it's not as noticeable.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Use a cotton swab soaked with hydrogen peroxide as a last resort. If you still have some dye on your carpet that won't come out and is pretty obvious, hydrogen peroxide will take care of it. Dip a cotton swab in hydrogen peroxide, then press it into the spot. You might need to do this several times so that the spot is completely saturated.<sup id=\"_ref-18\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 18\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-18\">[18]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-18.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 18.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/4e/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-18.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-18.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Hydrogen peroxide might also take the color out of your carpet, but if you have a white or light beige carpet, that might not be as noticeable as the hair dye stain.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Rinse hydrogen peroxide out of the carpet after a day. You might have to leave the hydrogen peroxide on the stain for up to 24 hours to make sure you've gotten rid of the stain. When you can no longer see the stain, rinse the area with cool water to get any remaining hydrogen peroxide out of the carpet.<sup id=\"_ref-19\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 19\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-19\">[19]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-19.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Remove Permanent Hair Dye from Carpets Step 19.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/b6/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-19.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-19.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>Since you didn't use a lot of hydrogen peroxide, you likely won't need a lot of water to rinse. Use a dry sponge or cloth to soak up the water after you've rinsed.</li>\n   </ul></li>\n </ol> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5\" title=\"Edit section: Tips\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Tips\">Tips</span></h2> \n <ul>\n  <li>Start cleaning up any dripped or spilled hair dye as soon as possible for the best results.</li> \n  <li>If the carpet is discolored or bleached out after you remove the dye, you can recolor it with a fabric pen.</li> \n  <li>If the hair dye stain is older and dried, these cleaning solutions might not work. Try a commercial carpet cleaning product or hire a professional carpet cleaner.<sup id=\"_ref-20\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 20\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-20\">[20]</a></sup></li>\n </ul> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6\" title=\"Edit section: Warnings\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Warnings\">Warnings</span></h2> \n <ul>\n  <li>Don't rub or scrub the stain — you'll only make it worse.<sup id=\"_ref-21\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 21\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets#_note-21\">[21]</a></sup></li>\n </ul> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7\" title=\"Edit section: Things You'll Need\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span id=\"Things-You'll-Need\"></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Things-You.27ll-Need\">Things You'll Need</span></h2> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8\" title=\"Edit section: Fresh Spills\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Fresh-Spills_2\">Fresh Spills</span></h3> \n <ul>\n  <li>Dishwashing liquid</li> \n  <li>White vinegar</li> \n  <li>Water</li> \n  <li>Clean, white cloths</li>\n </ul> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9\" title=\"Edit section: Older Stains\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Older-Stains\">Older Stains</span></h3> \n <ul>\n  <li>Dishwashing liquid</li> \n  <li>White vinegar</li> \n  <li>Water</li> \n  <li>Rubbing alcohol</li> \n  <li>Clean, white cloths</li>\n </ul> \n <h3><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10\" title=\"Edit section: Stubborn Spots\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Stubborn-Spots_2\">Stubborn Spots</span></h3> \n <ul>\n  <li>Dishwashing liquid</li> \n  <li>Ammonia</li> \n  <li>Water</li> \n  <li>Hydrogen peroxide</li> \n  <li>Cotton swabs</li> \n  <li>Clean, white cloths</li>\n </ul> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a delivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn91@2020_1/2020/10/12/17-04-49-249_b83b5d747e66623d.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/8/80/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-14.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-14.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn31@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-47-337_ef1a1bce116beaa9.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/c8/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-15.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-15.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx3/cdn36@2020_3/2020/10/12/17-04-49-441_2a37d5a45f590a22.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/3/31/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-16.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-16.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn95@2020_2/2020/10/12/17-04-47-321_95028faaa75e9f81.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/a/a1/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-17.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-17.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn55@2020_6/2020/10/12/17-04-47-253_6803d8f6120c66fa.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/4/4e/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-18.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-18.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn99@2020_4/2020/10/12/17-04-47-235_baf1d11e585ef571.webp","https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/b/b6/Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-19.jpg/aid2166793-v4-728px-Remove-Permanent-Hair-Dye-from-Carpets-Step-19.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx7/cdn77@2020_2/2020/10/12/17-04-47-214_e7250a62d61a970f.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1602522267308},{"createdTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:27","updatedTime":"2020-10-13 01:04:27","title":"How to Play a Video in a Zoom Meeting","link":"https://www.wikihow.com/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting","description":"<div class=\"mw-parser-output\">\n <p>This wikiHow will teach you how to play a video in a Zoom meeting so all the participants will see and hear it. It's a particularly useful tool for teachers presenting a video in a lesson. For the best results, you should use the desktop client to screen share your video. Using the mobile app to share video may result in the loss of audio. </p> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1\" title=\"Edit section: Steps\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Steps\">Steps</span></h2> \n <ol>\n  <li>Join or host a Zoom meeting. For more information on joining a meeting, refer to <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Join-a-Zoom-Meeting-on-PC-or-Mac\" title=\"Join a Zoom Meeting on PC or Mac\">How to Join a Zoom Meeting on PC or Mac</a>.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-1.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Play a Video in a Zoom Meeting Step 1.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/69/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-1.jpg/aid12172625-v4-728px-Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-1.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"545\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>If you want to host the meeting, open the desktop client, log in, and click <b>New Meeting </b>.</li>\n   </ul></li> \n  <li>Click . It's a green button centered at the bottom of the application window.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-2.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Play a Video in a Zoom Meeting Step 2.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/c/ca/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-2.jpg/aid12172625-v4-728px-Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-2.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"547\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Check the box next to \"Optimize Screen Sharing for Video Clip.<b>\"</b> When you click this box, the box next to \"Share computer sound\" checks off too, which will ensure your audience hears the video sound.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-3.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Play a Video in a Zoom Meeting Step 3.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/6/61/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-3.jpg/aid12172625-v4-728px-Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-3.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"548\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Click a window or application to share. You'll see all the screens you can share, including your Zoom screen and any tabs and windows you have open in a web browser, like YouTube.<sup id=\"_ref-1\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 1\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting#_note-1\">[1]</a></sup>\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-4.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Play a Video in a Zoom Meeting Step 4.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/1/1e/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-4.jpg/aid12172625-v4-728px-Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-4.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"547\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div></li> \n  <li>Click . Once you share the selected screen, the participants in the Zoom meeting will see what you've selected.\n   <div class=\"mwimg  largeimage  floatcenter \" style=\"max-width:728px\">\n    <a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Image:Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-5.jpg\" class=\"image\"><img alt=\"Play a Video in a Zoom Meeting Step 5.jpg\" src=\"https://www.wikihow.com/images/thumb/7/71/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-5.jpg/aid12172625-v4-728px-Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting-Step-5.jpg\" decoding=\"async\" width=\"728\" height=\"546\" class=\"whcdn\" /></a>\n   </div> \n   <ul>\n    <li>For example, if you selected a YouTube page in the previous step, the participants in the Zoom meeting will see the YouTube page in your web browser. You can click the full-screen icon in the bottom right corner of the YouTube video to make it full-screen.</li> \n    <li>When you want to stop sharing, click <b>Stop Share</b> at the top of your screen.<sup id=\"_ref-2\" class=\"reference\" aria-label=\"Link to Reference 2\"><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting#_note-2\">[2]</a></sup></li>\n   </ul></li>\n </ol> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">[</span><a target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.wikihow.com/index.php?title=Play-a-Video-in-a-Zoom-Meeting&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2\" title=\"Edit section: References\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"References\">References</span></h2> \n <h2><span class=\"mw-editsection\"><span Summary\">Edit</a><span class=\"mw-editsection-bracket\">]</span></span><span class=\"mw-headline\" id=\"Quick-Summary\">Quick Summary</span></h2>\n <div class=\"mw-references-wrap\">\n  <ol
